</uploaded_files>
I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Public unscoped enum constants not visible across module boundaries
**Issue Description**
After #7798, the constants in public unscoped enums are no longer visible across module boundaries, regardless of `public`.

**Reproducer Code**
```slang
// test_a.slang
[UnscopedEnum]
public enum TestEnum
{
    CASE_A,
    CASE_B
};
```

```slang
// test_b.slang
import test_a;

[numthreads(1, 1, 1)]
void computeMain(int3 dispatchThreadID: SV_DispatchThreadID)
{
    TestEnum e = CASE_A;
}
```

Compile with:
```
slangc -target spirv test_b.slang -o test.spv
```

Error message:
```
test_b.slang(6): error 30600: 'CASE_A' is not accessible from the current context.
    TestEnum e = CASE_A;
```

`TestEnum.CASE_A` is visible and if the enum is moved into `test_b.slang`, the unscoped `CASE_A` is also visible.

**Expected Behavior**
`CASE_A` is visible, as if it was in the same module.

**Actual Behavior**
Error message is given.

**Environment:**
 - Slang Version: a77d22bf3bfc3098b01e4886c3a63fb751edc704
 - OS: OpenSUSE Tumbleweed

**Additional context**
The PR that changed this behaviour is related to issue #7758, where it was mentioned that "canonical Slang code should always use scoped enums." Since modules are a Slang feature, it can also be entirely reasonable to ban unscoped enum visibility across module boundaries.

I have some code that currently uses this feature, but I'm working on moving it to scoped enums, so this issue is not at all a blocker for me. I was more just surprised that there was a change to the exisitng behaviour.

</pr_description>

Can you help me implement the necessary changes to the repository so that the requirements specified in the <pr_description> are met?

Your thinking should be thorough and so it's fine if it's very long.

     1	// slang-lookup.cpp
     2	#include "slang-lookup.h"
     3	
     4	#include "../compiler-core/slang-name.h"
     5	#include "slang-check-impl.h"
     6	
     7	// TODO(tfoley): The implementation of lookup still involves
     8	// recursion over the structure of a type/declaration, but
     9	// it should be possible for it to use the flattened/linearized
    10	// inheritance information that is being computed in
    11	// `slang-check-inheritance.cpp`.
    12	
    13	namespace Slang
    14	{
    15	
    16	void ensureDecl(SemanticsVisitor* visitor, Decl* decl, DeclCheckState state);
    17	
    18	//
    19	
    20	DeclRef<ExtensionDecl> applyExtensionToType(
    21	    SemanticsVisitor* semantics,
    22	    ExtensionDecl* extDecl,
    23	    Type* type);
    24	
    25	//
    26	
    27	
    28	// Helper for constructing breadcrumb trails during lookup, without unnecessary heap allocaiton
    29	struct BreadcrumbInfo
    30	{
    31	    LookupResultItem::Breadcrumb::Kind kind;
    32	    LookupResultItem::Breadcrumb::ThisParameterMode thisParameterMode =
    33	        LookupResultItem::Breadcrumb::ThisParameterMode::Default;
    34	    DeclRef<Decl> declRef;
    35	    Val* val = nullptr;
    36	    BreadcrumbInfo* prev = nullptr;
    37	};
    38	
    39	//
    40	
    41	bool DeclPassesLookupMask(Decl* decl, LookupMask mask)
    42	{
    43	    // Always exclude extern members from lookup result.
    44	    if (decl->hasModifier<ExtensionExternVarModifier>())
    45	    {
    46	        return false;
    47	    }
    48	    else if (decl->hasModifier<ExternModifier>())
    49	    {
    50	        if (as<ExtensionDecl>(decl->parentDecl))
    51	        {
    52	            return false;
    53	        }
    54	    }
    55	    // type declarations
    56	    if (const auto aggTypeDecl = as<AggTypeDecl>(decl))
    57	    {
    58	        return int(mask) & int(LookupMask::type);
    59	    }
    60	    else if (const auto simpleTypeDecl = as<SimpleTypeDecl>(decl))
    61	    {
    62	        return int(mask) & int(LookupMask::type);
    63	    }
    64	    // function declarations
    65	    else if (const auto funcDecl = as<FunctionDeclBase>(decl))
    66	    {
    67	        return (int(mask) & int(LookupMask::Function)) != 0;
    68	    }
    69	    // attribute declaration
    70	    else if (const auto attrDecl = as<AttributeDecl>(decl))
    71	    {
    72	        return (int(mask) & int(LookupMask::Attribute)) != 0;
    73	    }
    74	    // syntax declaration
    75	    else if (const auto syntaxDecl = as<SyntaxDecl>(decl))
    76	    {
    77	        return (int(mask) & int(LookupMask::SyntaxDecl)) != 0;
    78	    }
    79	    // default behavior is to assume a value declaration
    80	    // (no overloading allowed)
    81	
    82	    return (int(mask) & int(LookupMask::Value)) != 0;
    83	}
    84	
    85	void AddToLookupResult(LookupResult& result, LookupResultItem item)
    86	{
    87	    if (!result.isValid())
    88	    {
    89	        // If we hadn't found a hit before, we have one now
    90	        result.item = item;
    91	    }
    92	    else if (!result.isOverloaded())
    93	    {
    94	        // We are about to make this overloaded
    95	        result.items.add(result.item);
    96	        result.items.add(item);
    97	    }
    98	    else
    99	    {
   100	        // The result was already overloaded, so we pile on
   101	        result.items.add(item);
   102	    }
   103	}
   104	
   105	void AddToLookupResult(LookupResult& result, const LookupResult& items)
   106	{
   107	    if (items.isOverloaded())
   108	    {
   109	        for (auto item : items.items)
   110	            AddToLookupResult(result, item);
   111	    }
   112	    else if (items.isValid())
   113	    {
   114	        AddToLookupResult(result, items.item);
   115	    }
   116	}
   117	
   118	LookupResult refineLookup(LookupResult const& inResult, LookupMask mask)
   119	{
   120	    if (!inResult.isValid())
   121	        return inResult;
   122	    if (!inResult.isOverloaded())
   123	        return inResult;
   124	
   125	    LookupResult result;
   126	    for (auto item : inResult.items)
   127	    {
   128	        if (!DeclPassesLookupMask(item.declRef.getDecl(), mask))
   129	            continue;
   130	
   131	        AddToLookupResult(result, item);
   132	    }
   133	    return result;
   134	}
   135	
   136	LookupResultItem CreateLookupResultItem(DeclRef<Decl> declRef, BreadcrumbInfo* breadcrumbInfos)
   137	{
   138	    LookupResultItem item;
   139	    item.declRef = declRef;
   140	
   141	    // breadcrumbs were constructed "backwards" on the stack, so we
   142	    // reverse them here by building a linked list the other way
   143	    RefPtr<LookupResultItem::Breadcrumb> breadcrumbs;
   144	    for (auto bb = breadcrumbInfos; bb; bb = bb->prev)
   145	    {
   146	        breadcrumbs = new LookupResultItem::Breadcrumb(
   147	            bb->kind,
   148	            bb->declRef,
   149	            bb->val,
   150	            breadcrumbs,
   151	            bb->thisParameterMode);
   152	    }
   153	    item.breadcrumbs = breadcrumbs;
   154	    return item;
   155	}
   156	
   157	static void _lookUpMembersInValue(
   158	    ASTBuilder* astBuilder,
   159	    Name* name,
   160	    DeclRef<Decl> valueDeclRef,
   161	    LookupRequest const& request,
   162	    LookupResult& ioResult,
   163	    BreadcrumbInfo* breadcrumbs);
   164	
   165	static bool _isUncheckedLocalVar(const Decl* decl)
   166	{
   167	    auto checkStateExt = decl->checkState;
   168	    auto isUnchecked = checkStateExt.getState() == DeclCheckState::Unchecked ||
   169	                       checkStateExt.isBeingChecked() || decl->hiddenFromLookup;
   170	    return isUnchecked && isLocalVar(decl);
   171	}
   172	
   173	/// Look up direct members (those declared in `containerDeclRef` itself, as well
   174	/// as transitively through any direct members that are marked "transparent."
   175	///
   176	/// This function does *not* deal with looking up through `extension`s,
   177	/// inheritance clauses, etc.
   178	///
   179	static void _lookUpDirectAndTransparentMembers(
   180	    ASTBuilder* astBuilder,
   181	    Name* name,
   182	    ContainerDecl* containerDecl, // The container decl to find member with `name`.
   183	    DeclRef<Decl> parentDeclRef,  // The parent of the resulting declref.
   184	    LookupRequest const& request,
   185	    LookupResult& result,
   186	    BreadcrumbInfo* inBreadcrumbs)
   187	{
   188	    if (request.isCompletionRequest())
   189	    {
   190	        // If we are looking up for completion suggestions,
   191	        // return all the members that are available.
   192	        for (auto member : containerDecl->getDirectMemberDecls())
   193	        {
   194	            if (!request.shouldConsiderAllLocalNames() && _isUncheckedLocalVar(member))
   195	                continue;
   196	            if (!DeclPassesLookupMask(member, request.mask))
   197	                continue;
   198	            AddToLookupResult(
   199	                result,
   200	                CreateLookupResultItem(

 11731	
 11732	void SemanticsDeclScopeWiringVisitor::visitNamespaceDecl(NamespaceDecl* decl)
 11733	{
 11734	    // We need to wire up the scope of namespaces with other namespace decls of the same name
 11735	    // that is accessible from the current context.
 11736	    auto parent = as<ContainerDecl>(getParentDecl(decl));
 11737	    if (!parent)
 11738	        return;
 11739	    for (auto parentScope = parent->ownedScope; parentScope; parentScope = parentScope->parent)
 11740	    {
 11741	        for (auto scope = parentScope; scope; scope = scope->nextSibling)
 11742	        {
 11743	            auto container = scope->containerDecl;
 11744	            auto nsDecl = container->findLastDirectMemberDeclOfName(decl->getName());
 11745	            if (!nsDecl)
 11746	                continue;
 11747	            for (auto ns = nsDecl; ns; ns = container->getPrevDirectMemberDeclWithSameName(ns))
 11748	            {
 11749	                if (ns == decl)
 11750	                    continue;
 11751	                auto otherNamespace = as<NamespaceDeclBase>(ns);
 11752	                if (!otherNamespace)
 11753	                    continue;
 11754	
 11755	                if (!ns->checkState.isBeingChecked())
 11756	                {
 11757	                    ensureDecl(ns, DeclCheckState::ScopesWired);
 11758	                }
 11759	                addSiblingScopeForContainerDecl(getASTBuilder(), decl, otherNamespace);
 11760	            }
 11761	        }
 11762	        // For file decls, we need to continue searching up in the parent module scope.
 11763	        if (!as<FileDecl>(parentScope->containerDecl))
 11764	            break;
 11765	    }
 11766	    for (auto usingDecl : decl->getMembersOfType<UsingDecl>())
 11767	    {
 11768	        ensureDecl(usingDecl, DeclCheckState::ScopesWired);
 11769	    }
 11770	}

 11774	/// Note: this function creates an empty list of candidates for the given type if

 11777	static List<ExtensionDecl*>& _getCandidateExtensionList(

 11783	    {
 11784	        entry = new CandidateExtensionList();
 11785	        mapTypeToCandidateExtensions.add(typeDecl, entry);
 11786	    }

  1000	LookupResult SemanticsVisitor::filterLookupResultByVisibility(const LookupResult& lookupResult)
  1001	{
  1002	    if (!m_outerScope)
  1003	        return lookupResult;
  1004	    LookupResult filteredResult;
  1005	    for (auto item : lookupResult)
  1006	    {
  1007	        if (isDeclVisibleFromScope(item.declRef, m_outerScope))

  1017	{
  1018	    outDiagnosed = false;
  1019	    auto result = filterLookupResultByVisibility(lookupResult);
  1020	    if (lookupResult.isValid() && !result.isValid())
  1021	    {
  1022	        getSink()->diagnose(loc, Diagnostics::declIsNotVisible, lookupResult.item.declRef);
  1023	        outDiagnosed = true;
  1024	
  1025	        if (getShared()->isInLanguageServer())
  1026	        {
  1027	            // When in language server mode, return the unfiltered result so we can still
  1028	            // provide language service around it.
  1029	            return lookupResult;
  1030	        }
  1031	    }
  1032	    return result;
  1033	}
  1034	
  1035	bool SemanticsVisitor::isWitnessUncheckedOptional(SubtypeWitness* witness)
  1036	{
  1037	    auto declaredWitness = as<DeclaredSubtypeWitness>(witness);
  1038	    if (!declaredWitness)
  1039	        return false;
  1040	
  1041	    auto decl = declaredWitness->getDeclRef().getDecl();
  1042	    if (!decl || !decl->hasModifier<OptionalConstraintModifier>())
  1043	        return false;
  1044	
  1045	    // Okay, we've found an optional subtype witness. This result needs
  1046	    // to be removed if we're not inside a block that directly checks
  1047	    // if (sub is sup)
  1048	    auto sub = witness->getSub();
  1049	    auto sup = witness->getSup();
  1050

   960	        }
   961	        return v;
   962	    }
   963	    return DeclVisibility::Public;
   964	}
   965	
   966	bool SemanticsVisitor::isDeclVisibleFromScope(DeclRef<Decl> declRef, Scope* scope)
   967	{
   968	    auto visibility = getDeclVisibility(declRef.getDecl());
   969	    if (visibility == DeclVisibility::Public)
   970	        return true;
   971	    if (visibility == DeclVisibility::Internal)
   972	    {
   973	        // Check that the decl is in the same module as the scope.
   974	        auto declModule = getModuleDecl(declRef.getDecl());
   975	        if (declModule == getModuleDecl(scope))
   976	            return true;
   977	    }
   978	    if (visibility == DeclVisibility::Private)
   979	    {
   980	        // Check that the decl is in the same or parent container decl as scope.
   981	        Decl* parentContainer = declRef.getDecl();
   982	        for (; parentContainer; parentContainer = parentContainer->parentDecl)
   983	        {
   984	            if (as<AggTypeDeclBase>(parentContainer))
   985	                break;
   986	            if (as<NamespaceDeclBase>(parentContainer))
   987	                break;
   988	        }
   989	
   990	        for (auto s = scope; s; s = s->parent)
   991	        {
   992	            if (s->containerDecl == parentContainer)
   993	                return true;
   994	        }
   995	        return false;
   996	    }
   997	    return false;
   998	}
   999

   179	static void _lookUpDirectAndTransparentMembers(
   180	    ASTBuilder* astBuilder,
   181	    Name* name,
   182	    ContainerDecl* containerDecl, // The container decl to find member with `name`.
   183	    DeclRef<Decl> parentDeclRef,  // The parent of the resulting declref.
   184	    LookupRequest const& request,
   185	    LookupResult& result,
   186	    BreadcrumbInfo* inBreadcrumbs)
   187	{
   188	    if (request.isCompletionRequest())
   189	    {
   190	        // If we are looking up for completion suggestions,
   191	        // return all the members that are available.
   192	        for (auto member : containerDecl->getDirectMemberDecls())
   193	        {
   194	            if (!request.shouldConsiderAllLocalNames() && _isUncheckedLocalVar(member))
   195	                continue;
   196	            if (!DeclPassesLookupMask(member, request.mask))
   197	                continue;
   198	            AddToLookupResult(
   199	                result,
   200	                CreateLookupResultItem(
   201	                    astBuilder->getMemberDeclRef<Decl>(parentDeclRef, member),
   202	                    inBreadcrumbs));
   203	        }
   204	    }
   205	    else
   206	    {
   207	        // Iterate over the declarations with the chosen name in the container
   208	        // (if any), and see if we find any that meet our filtering criteria.
   209	        //
   210	        // For example, we might be filtering so that we only consider
   211	        // type declarations.
   212	        //
   213	        for (auto m : containerDecl->getDirectMemberDeclsOfName(name))
   214	        {
   215	            // Skip this declaration if we are checking and this hasn't been
   216	            // checked yet. Because we traverse block statements in order, if
   217	            // it's unchecked or being checked then it isn't declared yet.
   218	            if (!request.shouldConsiderAllLocalNames() && request.semantics &&
   219	                _isUncheckedLocalVar(m))
   220	                continue;
   221	            if (m == request.declToExclude)
   222	                continue;
   223	
   224	            if (!DeclPassesLookupMask(m, request.mask))
   225	                continue;
   226	
   227	            // The declaration passed the test, so add it!
   228	            AddToLookupResult(
   229	                result,
   230	                CreateLookupResultItem(
   231	                    astBuilder->getMemberDeclRef<Decl>(parentDeclRef, m),
   232	                    inBreadcrumbs));
   233	        }
   234	    }
   235	
   236	    // Don't look up transparent members if we are looking for attributes, since
   237	    // they are always defined at global scope in the core module. Trying to lookup transparent
   238	    // members during attribute lookup can lead to infinite recursion on transparent types.
   239	    if ((int)request.mask & (int)LookupMask::Attribute)
   240	        return;
   241	
   242	    // Also skip transparent members if they're explicitly excluded by the
   243	    // request. This prevents cyclic lookups e.g. when looking up UnscopedEnum's
   244	    // underlying types.
   245	    if (((int)request.options & (int)LookupOptions::IgnoreTransparentMembers) != 0)
   246	        return;
   247	
   248	    for (auto transparentMemberDecl : containerDecl->getTransparentDirectMemberDecls())
   249	    {
   250	        // The reference to the transparent member should use the same

   251	        // path as we used in referring to its parent.
   252	        DeclRef<Decl> transparentMemberDeclRef =
   253	            astBuilder->getMemberDeclRef(parentDeclRef, transparentMemberDecl);
   254	        if (transparentMemberDeclRef.getDecl() == request.declToExclude)

   257	        // We need to leave a breadcrumb so that we know that the result
   258	        // of lookup involves a member lookup step here

   261	        memberRefBreadcrumb.kind = LookupResultItem::Breadcrumb::Kind::Member;

   266	            astBuilder,
   267	            name,
   268	            transparentMemberDeclRef,
   269	            request,
   270	            result,
   271	            &memberRefBreadcrumb);
   272	    }
   273	}

   291	        name == semantics->getSession()->getCompletionRequestTokenName())

   293

   214	void ContainerDeclDirectMemberDecls::_ensureLookupAcceleratorsAreValid() const
   215	{
   216	    if (_areLookupAcceleratorsValid())
   217	        return;
   218	
   219	    // If the `declCountWhenLastUpdated` is less than zero, it means that
   220	    // the accelerators are entirely invalidated, and must be rebuilt
   221	    // from scratch.
   222	    //
   223	    if (accelerators.declCountWhenLastUpdated < 0)
   224	    {
   225	        accelerators.declCountWhenLastUpdated = 0;
   226	        accelerators.mapNameToLastDeclOfThatName.clear();
   227	        accelerators.filteredListOfTransparentDecls.clear();
   228	    }
   229	
   230	    Count memberCount = decls.getCount();
   231	    Count memberCountWhenLastUpdated = accelerators.declCountWhenLastUpdated;
   232	
   233	    SLANG_ASSERT(memberCountWhenLastUpdated >= 0 && memberCountWhenLastUpdated <= memberCount);
   234	
   235	    // are we a generic?
   236	    GenericDecl* genericDecl = nullptr;
   237	    if (memberCount > 0)
   238	    {
   239	        genericDecl = as<GenericDecl>(decls[0]->parentDecl);
   240	    }
   241	
   242	    for (Index i = memberCountWhenLastUpdated; i < memberCount; ++i)
   243	    {
   244	        Decl* memberDecl = decls[i];
   245	
   246	        // Transparent member declarations will go into a separate list,
   247	        // so that they can be conveniently queried later for lookup
   248	        // operations.
   249	        //
   250	        // TODO: Rather than track these using a separate table, we
   251	        // could design a scheme where transparent members are put into
   252	        // the same lookup dictionary as everything else, just under
   253	        // a pseudo-name that identifies transparent members.
   254	        //
   255	        if (memberDecl->hasModifier<TransparentModifier>())
   256	        {
   257	            accelerators.filteredListOfTransparentDecls.add(memberDecl);
   258	        }
   259	
   260	        // Members that don't have a name don't go into the lookup dictionary.

  4865	static EnumDecl* isUnscopedEnum(Decl* decl)
  4866	{
  4867	    EnumDecl* enumDecl = as<EnumDecl>(decl);
  4868	    if (!enumDecl)
  4869	        return nullptr;
  4870	    for (auto mod : enumDecl->modifiers)
  4871	    {
  4872	        if (as<UnscopedEnumAttribute>(mod))
  4873	        {
  4874	            return enumDecl;
  4875	        }
  4876	        else if (auto uncheckedAttribute = as<UncheckedAttribute>(mod))
  4877	        {
  4878	            // We have to perform an ugly string comparison here, because the attributes
  4879	            // haven't been checked during parsing.
  4880	            if (getText(uncheckedAttribute->keywordName) == "UnscopedEnum")
  4881	            {
  4882	                return enumDecl;
  4883	            }
  4884	        }
  4885	    }
  4886	    return nullptr;
  4887	}

   950	DeclVisibility SemanticsVisitor::getTypeVisibility(Type* type)
   951	{
   952	    if (auto declRefType = as<DeclRefType>(type))
   953	    {
   954	        auto v = getDeclVisibility(declRefType->getDeclRef().getDecl());
   955	        auto args = findInnerMostGenericArgs(SubstitutionSet(declRefType->getDeclRef()));
   956	        for (auto arg : args)
   957	        {
   958	            if (auto typeArg = as<DeclRefType>(arg))
   959	                v = Math::Min(v, getTypeVisibility(typeArg));
   960	        }
   961	        return v;
   962	    }
   963	    return DeclVisibility::Public;
   964	}

 14624	DeclVisibility getDeclVisibility(Decl* decl)
 14625	{
 14626	    if (as<GenericTypeParamDeclBase>(decl) || as<GenericValueParamDecl>(decl) ||
 14627	        as<GenericTypeConstraintDecl>(decl))
 14628	    {
 14629	        auto genericDecl = as<GenericDecl>(decl->parentDecl);
 14630	        if (!genericDecl)
 14631	            return DeclVisibility::Default;
 14632	        if (genericDecl->inner)
 14633	            return getDeclVisibility(genericDecl->inner);
 14634	        return DeclVisibility::Default;
 14635	    }
 14636	    if (auto genericDecl = as<GenericDecl>(decl))
 14637	        decl = genericDecl->inner;
 14638	    for (; decl; decl = getParentDecl(decl))
 14639	    {
 14640	        if (as<AccessorDecl>(decl))
 14641	            continue;
 14642	        if (as<EnumCaseDecl>(decl))
 14643	            continue;
 14644	        break;
 14645	    }
 14646	    if (!decl)
 14647	        return DeclVisibility::Public;
 14648

 14650	    {
 14651	        if (as<PublicModifier>(modifier))
 14652	            return DeclVisibility::Public;
 14653	        else if (as<InternalModifier>(modifier))

   960	        }
   961	        return v;
   962	    }
   963	    return DeclVisibility::Public;
   964	}
   965	
   966	bool SemanticsVisitor::isDeclVisibleFromScope(DeclRef<Decl> declRef, Scope* scope)
   967	{
   968	    auto visibility = getDeclVisibility(declRef.getDecl());
   969	    if (visibility == DeclVisibility::Public)
   970	        return true;
   971	
   972	    // Special case for EnumCaseDecl of an UnscopedEnum.
   973	    // Their visibility should be the same as the EnumDecl.
   974	    if (auto enumCase = as<EnumCaseDecl>(declRef.getDecl()))
   975	    {
   976	        if (auto enumDecl = as<EnumDecl>(enumCase->parentDecl))
   977	        {
   978	            if (enumDecl->hasModifier<UnscopedEnumAttribute>())
   979	            {
   980	                if (getDeclVisibility(enumDecl) == DeclVisibility::Public)
   981	                    return true;
   982	            }
   983	        }
   984	    }
   985	
   986	    if (visibility == DeclVisibility::Internal)
   987	    {
   988	        // Check that the decl is in the same module as the scope.
   989	        auto declModule = getModuleDecl(declRef.getDecl());
   990	        if (declModule == getModuleDecl(scope))
   991	            return true;
   992	    }

   969	    if (visibility == DeclVisibility::Public)

   971	
   972	    // Special case for EnumCaseDecl of an UnscopedEnum.
   973	    // Their visibility should be the same as the EnumDecl.
   974	    if (auto letDecl = as<LetDecl>(declRef.getDecl()))

   976	        if (letDecl->initExpr)
   977	        {

   982	                    if (auto enumDecl = as<EnumDecl>(enumCase->parentDecl))
   983	                    {
   984	                        if (enumDecl->hasModifier<UnscopedEnumAttribute>())
   985	                        {
   986	                            if (getDeclVisibility(enumDecl) == DeclVisibility::Public)

  5574	static Decl* parseEnumDecl(Parser* parser)
  5575	{
  5576	    EnumDecl* decl = parser->astBuilder->create<EnumDecl>();
  5577	    parser->ReadToken("enum");
  5578	
  5579	    // HACK: allow the user to write `enum class` in case
  5580	    // they are trying to share a header between C++ and Slang.
  5581	    //
  5582	    // TODO: diagnose this with a warning some day, and move
  5583	    // toward deprecating it.
  5584	    //
  5585	    bool isEnumClass = AdvanceIf(parser, "class");
  5586	    bool isUnscoped = false;
  5587	
  5588	    if (!isEnumClass)
  5589	    {
  5590	        if (parser->options.optionSet.getBoolOption(CompilerOptionName::UnscopedEnum))
  5591	        {
  5592	            isUnscoped = true;
  5593	        }
  5594	    }
  5595	
  5596	    AdvanceIf(parser, TokenType::CompletionRequest);
  5597	
  5598	    parser->FillPosition(decl);
  5599	
  5600	    if (parser->tokenReader.peekTokenType() != TokenType::Identifier)
  5601	    {
  5602	        decl->nameAndLoc.name = generateName(parser);
  5603	        decl->nameAndLoc.loc = decl->loc;
  5604	        isUnscoped = true;
  5605	    }
  5606	    else
  5607	    {
  5608	        decl->nameAndLoc = expectIdentifier(parser);
  5609	    }
  5610	
  5611	
  5612	    return parseOptGenericDecl(
  5613	        parser,
  5614	        [&](GenericDecl* genericParent)
  5615	        {
  5616	            // If the type needs to be unscoped, insert modifiers to make it so.
  5617	            if (isUnscoped && !genericParent)
  5618	            {
  5619	                addModifier(decl, parser->astBuilder->create<UnscopedEnumAttribute>());
  5620	            }
  5621	            parseOptionalInheritanceClause(parser, decl);
  5622	            maybeParseGenericConstraints(parser, genericParent);
  5623	            parser->ReadToken(TokenType::LBrace);
  5624	            Token closingToken;
  5625	            parser->pushScopeAndSetParent(decl);
  5626	            while (!AdvanceIfMatch(parser, MatchedTokenType::CurlyBraces, &closingToken))
  5627	            {
  5628	                EnumCaseDecl* caseDecl = parseEnumCaseDecl(parser);
  5629	                AddMember(decl, caseDecl);
  5630	
  5631	                if (AdvanceIf(parser, TokenType::RBrace))
  5632	                    break;
  5633	
  5634	                parser->ReadToken(TokenType::Comma);
  5635	            }
  5636	            parser->PopScope();
  5637	            decl->closingSourceLoc = closingToken.loc;
  5638	            return decl;
  5639	        });
  5640	}
  5641	
  5642	static Stmt* ParseSwitchStmt(Parser* parser)
  5643	{
  5644	    SwitchStmt* stmt = parser->astBuilder->create<SwitchStmt>();
  5645	    parser->FillPosition(stmt);
  5646	    parser->ReadToken("switch");
  5647	    parser->ReadToken(TokenType::LParent);
  5648	    stmt->condition = parser->ParseExpression();
  5649	    parser->ReadToken(TokenType::RParent);
  5650	    stmt->body = parser->parseBlockStatement();

    20	// Helper class useful to build a list of modifiers.
    21	struct ModifierListBuilder
    22	{
    23	    ModifierListBuilder() { m_next = &m_result; }
    24	    void add(Modifier* modifier)
    25	    {
    26	        // Doesn't handle SharedModifiers
    27	        SLANG_ASSERT(as<SharedModifiers>(modifier) == nullptr);
    28	
    29	        // Splice at end
    30	        *m_next = modifier;
    31	        m_next = &modifier->next;
    32	    }
    33	    template<typename T>
    34	    T* find() const
    35	    {
    36	        Modifier* cur = m_result;
    37	        while (cur)
    38	        {
    39	            T* castCur = as<T>(cur);
    40	            if (castCur)
    41	            {
    42	                return castCur;
    43	            }
    44	            cur = cur->next;
    45	        }
    46	        return nullptr;
    47	    }
    48	    template<typename T>
    49	    bool hasType() const
    50	    {
    51	        return find<T>() != nullptr;
    52	    }
    53	    Modifier* getFirst() { return m_result; };
    54	
    55	protected:
    56	    Modifier* m_result = nullptr;
    57	    Modifier** m_next;
    58	};

   966	bool SemanticsVisitor::isDeclVisibleFromScope(DeclRef<Decl> declRef, Scope* scope)
   967	{
   968	    if (visibility == DeclVisibility::Public)
   969	        return true;
   970	
   971	    if (visibility == DeclVisibility::Internal)
   972	    {
   973	        // Check that the decl is in the same module as the scope.
   974	        auto declModule = getModuleDecl(declRef.getDecl());
   975	        if (declModule == getModuleDecl(scope))
   976	            return true;
   977	    }
   978	    if (visibility == DeclVisibility::Private)
   979	    {
   980	        // Check that the decl is in the same or parent container decl as scope.
   981	        Decl* parentContainer = declRef.getDecl();
   982	        for (; parentContainer; parentContainer = parentContainer->parentDecl)
   983	        {
   984	            if (as<AggTypeDeclBase>(parentContainer))
   985	                break;
   986	            if (as<NamespaceDeclBase>(parentContainer))
   987	                break;
   988	        }
   989	
   990	        for (auto s = scope; s; s = s->parent)
   991	        {
   992	            if (s->containerDecl == parentContainer)
   993	                return true;
   994	        }
   995	    }
   996	    return false;
   997	}
   998	
   999	LookupResult SemanticsVisitor::filterLookupResultByVisibility(const LookupResult& lookupResult)
  1000	{
  1001	    if (!m_outerScope)
  1002	        return lookupResult;
  1003	    LookupResult filteredResult;
  1004	    for (auto item : lookupResult)
  1005	    {
  1006	        if (isDeclVisibleFromScope(item.declRef, m_outerScope))
  1007	            AddToLookupResult(filteredResult, item);
  1008	    }
  1009	    return filteredResult;
  1010	}

{
    auto visibility = getDeclVisibility(declRef.getDecl());
    if (visibility == DeclVisibility::Public)
        return true;

    // Special case for EnumCaseDecl of an UnscopedEnum.
    // Their visibility should be the same as the EnumDecl.
    if (auto letDecl = as<LetDecl>(declRef.getDecl()))
    {
        if (letDecl->initExpr)
        {
            if (auto varExpr = as<VarExpr>(letDecl->initExpr))
            {
                if (auto enumCase = as<EnumCaseDecl>(varExpr->declRef.getDecl()))
                {
                    if (auto enumDecl = as<EnumDecl>(enumCase->parentDecl))
                    {
                        if (enumDecl->hasModifier<UnscopedEnumAttribute>())
                        {
                            if (isDeclVisibleFromScope(DeclRef<Decl>(enumDecl), scope))
                                return true;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        {
            if (enumDecl->hasModifier<UnscopedEnumAttribute>())
